# <a name="office-365-operated-by-21vianet"></a><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-104">由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-104">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-p102">由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365，是設計用以滿足在中國對於安全性、可靠性和可調整性雲端服務的需求。這項服務由 Microsoft 授權給 21Vianet 的技術提供支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-p102">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet is designed to meet the needs for secure, reliable, and scalable cloud services in China. This service is powered by technology that Microsoft has licensed to 21Vianet.</span></span>
  
>[!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-107">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-107">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span><br/> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-p103">Microsoft 不直接營運此項服務。由 21Vianet 營運、提供並管理服務的提供。21Vianet 是中國最大的運營商中立網際網路資料中心服務提供者，提供託管、受管理的網路服務，以及雲端運算基礎結構服務。透過 Microsoft 授權的技術，21Vianet 會營運當地的 Office 365 資料中心，以提供 Office 365 服務，並將資料保留在中國境內。21Vianet 也提供[訂閱和計費服務以及支援](https://docs.microsoft.com/Office365/Admin/contact-support-for-business-products?view=o365-21vianet&tabs=phone)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-p103">Microsoft does not operate the service itself. 21Vianet operates, provides, and manages delivery of the service. 21Vianet is the largest carrier-neutral Internet data center services provider in China, providing hosting, managed network services, and cloud computing infrastructure services. By licensing Microsoft technologies, 21Vianet operates local Office 365 datacenters to provide the ability to use Office 365 services while keeping data within China. 21Vianet also provides [subscription and billing services, as well as support](https://docs.microsoft.com/Office365/Admin/contact-support-for-business-products?view=o365-21vianet&tabs=phone).</span></span>
  
>[!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-113">這些服務須遵守中國法律。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-113">These services are subject to Chinese laws.</span></span><br/> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-p104">由於中國服務的獨特本質 (由合作夥伴從中國內部的資料中心營運)，可能尚未啟用部分功能。經過一段時間後，客戶將會看到服務的功能逐漸完整。有關的差異，請參閱服務描述註腳。如需更高層級的差異概觀，請參閱[深入了解由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-p104">Due to the unique nature of the China services—operated by a partner from datacenters inside China—there are some features that have not yet been enabled. Customers will see the services come closer to full feature parity over time. See the service description footnotes for differences. For a higher-level overview of differences, see [Learn about Office 365 operated by 21Vianet](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china).</span></span>
  
## <a name="service-availability-within-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-118">每個方案中可用的服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-118">Service availability within each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-p105">每個由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 方案皆包含一些個別服務，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。下表顯示每項 Office 365 方案中可用的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-p105">Each Office 365 plan operated by 21Vianet includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online. The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>
  
>[!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-p106">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-p106">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China. </span></span><br/>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1138"><sup>1</sup> 由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 和 Office 365 不支援任何不受製造商支援的作業系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1138"><sup>1</sup>Office 365 and Office 365 operated by 21Vianet do not provide support for any operating system that is not supported by its manufacturer.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1139"><sup>2</sup> 由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 企業版 F1 中，Office 365 影片僅限檢視 (不可發佈或共用)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1139"><sup>2</sup> In Office 365 Enterprise F1 operated by 21Vianet, Office 365 Video is limited to viewing only (no publishing or sharing).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1140"><sup>3</sup> 若您正在透過本機 Active Directory 使用目錄同步作業，則必須使用本機 Active Directory (而非透過 Office 365 入口網站) 或適用於 Windows PowerShell 的 Azure Active Directory 模組來刪除帳戶或變更密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1140"><sup>3</sup> If using directory synchronization with a local Active Directory, you must delete accounts or change passwords by using the local Active Directory, rather than the Office 365 portal or by using the Azure Active Directory module for Windows PowerShell.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1142"><sup>5</sup> 您僅能有一個 Office 365 公用網站，除非您已從 Office 365 的較舊版本進行升級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1142"><sup>5</sup> You can have only one Public Website with Office 365, unless you've upgraded from an earlier version of Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1143">如果您已升級，則可代管兩個共用網站，但僅其中一個可使用自訂網域名稱進行代管。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1143">In that case, you have two Public Websites, but only one of them can be hosted with a custom domain name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1144">For more information about working with the two websites for Business subscriptions, see [Work with your two Office 365 Public Websites](https://support.office.com/article/Use-a-public-website-with-Office-365-a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1144">For more information about working with the two websites for Business subscriptions, see [Work with your two Office 365 Public Websites](https://support.office.com/article/Use-a-public-website-with-Office-365-a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1145">If you have a different subscription, learn more about public websites at [Public Website help for Office 365](https://support.office.com/article/Use-a-public-website-with-Office-365-a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1145">If you have a different subscription, learn more about public websites at [Public Website help for Office 365](https://support.office.com/article/Use-a-public-website-with-Office-365-a8178510-501d-4bd8-9921-b04f2e9517a5).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1146"><sup>6</sup> 若減少以折扣條件購買的基座，有可能需支付提前終止訂閱的費用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1146"><sup>6</sup> Reducing seats that were purchased with a term discount may be subject to an early termination fee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1147">這不適用於每月付款的訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1147">This is not applicable for subscriptions paid on a monthly basis.</span></span><br/>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1716"><sup>1</sup> 此版本的 Office 支援封存和相容性功能，但不包含 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online 方案，且必須另外購買或搭配支援的同等內部部署伺服器使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1716"><sup>1</sup> Archiving and compliance features are supported with this version of Office, but the Exchange Online and SharePoint Online plans are not included and must be purchased separately or used with supported on-premises server equivalents.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1717"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1717"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1718"><sup>3</sup> 如果您有 Office Professional Plus 2013 或獨立版本的 Excel 2013，則可以下載 [適用於 Excel 2013 的 Power Map 預覽版](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=38395&amp;clcid=0x409)，並當作不受支援的增益集使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1718"><sup>3</sup> If you have Office Professional Plus 2013 or a standalone version of Excel 2013, you can download and use the [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=38395&amp;clcid=0x409) as an unsupported add-in.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1719"><sup>4</sup> 所有客戶皆可使用商務用 Skype 基本版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1719"><sup>4</sup>Skype for Business Basic is available for all customers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1720">商務用 Skype 桌面用戶端是在本機安裝的應用程式，可針對包含 商務用 Skype Online 的 Office 365 方案，提供目前狀態、立即訊息和會議功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1720">The Skype for Business desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1721">Office 365 專業增強版 和 Office 365 Enterprise E3 包含完整的 Skype 應用程式，其包含額外的功能，例如：進階電話語音支援、封存和法規遵循功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1721">Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Enterprise E3 include the full Skype application, which includes additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1722">必須為每個使用者指派商務用 Skype Online 授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1722">A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1723">如需有關 Lync 基本功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[桌面用戶端比較表](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1723">For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Skype for Business Online client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables).</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1724"><sup>5</sup> 部分學校符合教育增強版的資格，其包含 Office 365 專業增強版，可讓學生和教職員在最多五部 PC 或 Mac 電腦及其他行動裝置 (包含 Windows 平版電腦及 iPad) 上安裝最新版的 Office。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1724"><sup>5</sup> Some schools are eligible for Education Plus, which includes Office 365 ProPlus, and allows students, faculty and staff to install the latest version of Office on up to five PC or Mac computers and on other mobile devices, including Windows tablets and the iPad.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1725">當學校透過註冊教育版解決方案、Open Value Subscription 教育版解決方案或學校合約，為全機構的教職人員授權 Office 時，學校即符合 Office 365 教育增強版的資格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1725">Schools qualify for Office 365 Education Plus when they license Office institution-wide for faculty and staff through Enrollment for Education Solutions, Open Value Subscription Education Solutions, or a school contract.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1726">請注意，Access 和 Publisher 僅在 PC 上可供使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1726">Note that Access and Publisher are available on PCs only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1727">OneNote for Mac 可分別從 Mac App Store 下載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1727">OneNote for Mac is available as a separate download from the Mac App Store.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1728"><sup>6</sup> 可安裝 Mac 版 Office 2011，但不可啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1728"><sup>6</sup> Office 2011 for Mac can be installed, but not activated.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1729"><sup>7</sup>Office 365 ProPlus 在使用者專用的虛擬桌面基礎結構 (VDI) 上受支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1729"><sup>7</sup>Office 365 ProPlus is supported on user-dedicated virtual desktop infrastructure (VDI).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1730">當透過大量授權方案購買時，Office 365 ProPlus 僅支援遠端桌面服務 (RDS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1730">Office 365 ProPlus only supports Remote Desktop Services (RDS) when purchased through a Volume Licensing Program.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1731"><sup>8</sup>Office 365 Enterprise E3 和 Office 365 專業增強版 的大量啟用僅限於在 Windows Server 2008 R2 與更新版本上的安裝，且須啟用 RDS 角色或 Windows To Go 安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1731"><sup>8</sup> Volume activation for Office 365 Enterprise E3 and Office 365 ProPlus are limited to installations on Windows Server 2008 R2 and newer with the RDS role enabled or Windows To Go installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1732">在任一情況下，存取這些安裝程式的使用者必須是 Office365 企業版 E3，或Office 365 ProPlus 的授權使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1732">In either case, users accessing these installations need to be licensed users of Office 365 Enterprise E3 or Office 365 ProPlus.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1733"><sup>9</sup> 如果您在目前通道或目標發行的順延通道上，則目前即可使用 Access。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1733"><sup>9</sup> Access is currently available if you're on Current Channel or on Targeted release for Deferred Channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1734">如果您在順延通道上，則可在 2017 年 6 月存取 Access。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1734">If you're on Deferred Channel, Access will be available in June 2017.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1735">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Access 隨附在 Office 365 商務版和商務進階版中](https://support.office.com/article/Access-included-as-part-of-Office-365-Business-and-Business-Premium-f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1735">For more information, see [Access included as part of Office 365 Business and Business Premium](https://support.office.com/article/Access-included-as-part-of-Office-365-Business-and-Business-Premium-f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1736"><sup>10</sup> Visio Online 目前正由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 進行預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1736"><sup>10</sup> Visio Online is currently in preview for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1737">如需 Visio Online 的詳細資訊，請參閱[Visio Online 服務說明 (翻譯說明)](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1737">For more information about Visio Online, see the [Visio Online Service Description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1739"><sup>15</sup> 無法在中國取得 Google 服務 (包括 Play 商店)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1739"><sup>15</sup> Google services (including Play Store) are not accessible inside China.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1740">使用者可以從幾個由主要電話製造商或搜尋引擎公司維護的網路程式商店，安裝行動應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1740">There are several app stores maintained by major phone manufacturers or search engine companies that users can install mobile apps from.</span></span>
  
## <a name="office-for-the-web-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-1741">網頁版 Office 的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-1741">Office for the web features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2565"><sup>1</sup> 部分協力廠商的 Web 組件和增益集可能無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2565">Some third-party web parts and add-ins may not be available.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2566"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2566"><sup>2</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2567"><sup>3</sup>傳輸規則由彈性準則構成，可讓您定義條件和例外狀況，以及根據準則採取的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2567">Transport rules are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions and exceptions, and actions to take based on the criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2568">MO_ExchangeOnline 和 Microsoft ExchangeServer2013 之間可用的準則和動作並不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2568">The available criteria and actions differ between Exchange Online, and Microsoft Exchange Server 2013.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2569">如需可用準則和動作的清單，請參閱每一個產品對應的準則和動作主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2569">For a list of available criteria and actions, see the corresponding criteria and actions topics for each product.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2570"><sup>4</sup> 只能透過直接存取 Exchange 系統管理中心 (EAC) 管理介面進行存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2570">Only accessible via direct access to the Exchange admin center (EAC) management interface.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2700"><sup>1</sup> 郵件使用者會定義為「信箱」，而且可以連同外部郵件連絡人直接在 Exchange 系統管理中心 (EAC) 中新增、移除或管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2700"><sup>1</sup> Mail users are defined as "Mailboxes," and, along with external mail contacts, can be added, removed, and otherwise managed directly in the Exchange admin center (EAC).</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2701"> 
<sup>2</sup> 沒有 RBAC 自訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2701"> 
<sup>2</sup> No RBAC customization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2702">僅限系統管理員角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2702">Admin roles only.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2703"><sup>3</sup> 可在 EAC 中檢視受管理網域，並編輯網域類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2703"><sup>3</sup> Managed domains can be viewed and domain types can be edited in the EAC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2704">其他所有網域管理作業必須在 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2704">All other domain management must be done in the Office 365 admin center.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2705"> 
<sup>4</sup> EOP 與 Exchange Online 可用的彈性準則和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2705"> 
<sup>4</sup> The available flexible criteria and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2706">如需 EOP 中可用的準則和動作清單，請參閱 [傳輸規則準則](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/exchange-online-protection-service-description/messaging-policy-and-compliance-servicedesc)和[傳輸規則動作](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/policy-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/actions?view=exchserver-2019)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2706">For a list of available criteria and actions in EOP, see [Transport Rule Criteria](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/exchange-online-protection-service-description/messaging-policy-and-compliance-servicedesc) and [Transport Rule Actions](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/policy-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/actions?view=exchserver-2019).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2707">如需 Exchange Online 中可用的準則和動作清單，請參閱[傳輸規則準則](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions)和[傳輸規則動作](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2707">For a list of available criteria and actions in Exchange Online, see [Transport Rule Criteria](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions) and [Transport Rule Actions](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions).</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2708">

<sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2709"> 
<sup>6</sup> 預設的內容篩選動作，就是將垃圾郵件移至收件者的 [垃圾郵件] 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2709"> 
<sup>6</sup> The default content filter action is to move spam messages to the recipients' Junk Email folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2710">若要讓此動作能在內部部署信箱中運作，您還必須在內部部署伺服器上設定兩個 Exchange 傳輸規則，以偵測 EOP 所新增的垃圾郵件標頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2710">For this to work with on-premises mailboxes, you must also configure two Exchange Transport rules on your on-premises servers to detect spam headers added by EOP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2711">如需詳細資訊，請參閱＜ [確定垃圾郵件路由傳送至每一個使用者的垃圾郵件資料夾](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/SecurityCompliance/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder)＞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2711">For more information, see [Ensure that Spam is Routed to Each User's Junk Email Folder](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/SecurityCompliance/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder).</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2712"> 
<sup>7</sup> 透過 EOP 篩選其信箱的 Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) 客戶可以使用此功能，而且很快就可以供 Exchange Online 客戶使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2712"> 
<sup>7</sup> This feature is available to Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) customers whose mailboxes are being filtered by EOP, and will soon be available to Exchange Online customers.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2713"> 
<sup>8</sup> EOP 報告是 Exchange Online 報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2713"> 
<sup>8</sup> EOP reports are a subset of Exchange Online reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2714"><sup>9</sup> 包括 DLP 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2714"><sup>9</sup> Includes DLP reports.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2715"> 
<sup>10</sup> 會掃描輸入及輸出郵件，但不掃描從組織中寄件者傳送給組織中收件者的內部郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2715"> 
<sup>10</sup> Scans inbound and outbound messages, but does not scan internal messages sent from a sender in your organization to a recipient in your organization.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2716"><sup>11</sup> EOP 與 Exchange Online 可用的述詞和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2716"><sup>11</sup> The available predicates and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2717"> 
<sup>12</sup> 混合式安裝程式不能透過混合式精靈使用，但您可以手動設定 (如果您有 Exchange SP1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2717"> 
<sup>12</sup> Hybrid setup is not available through Hybrid Wizard, but can be set up manually if you have Exchange SP1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2792"><sup>1</sup> 使用者信箱必須位於 Exchange 2010 SP2 或更新版本上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2792"><sup>1</sup> User mailboxes must reside on Exchange 2010 SP2 or later.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2793"><sup>2</sup> 「就地封存」僅可用來封存已套用授權之單一使用者或實體的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2793"><sup>2</sup> In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity for which a license has been applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2794">禁止使用「就地封存」來儲存多個使用者或實體的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2794">Using an In-Place Archive as a means to store mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2795">例如，IT 系統管理員不能建立共用信箱，再由使用者純粹為了封存的目的來複製 (透過 [副本] 或 [密件副本] 欄位，或透過傳輸規則) 共用信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2795">For example, IT administrators can't create shared mailboxes and have users copy (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a transport rule) a shared mailbox for the explicit purpose of archiving.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2796"> 
<sup>3</sup> 如需支援的 Microsoft Outlook 版本清單，請參閱 [Exchange Online 封存中的用戶端功能](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2796"> 
<sup>3</sup> For a list of supported Microsoft Outlook versions see [Client Features in Exchange Online Archiving](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md).</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2797"> 
<sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2797"> 
<sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2798"> 
<sup>5</sup> 當您對信箱進行就地保留或訴訟資料暫留時，會同時保留主要和封存信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2798"> 
<sup>5</sup> When you put a mailbox on In-Place Hold or Litigation Hold, the hold is placed on both the primary and the archive mailbox.</span></span> 
  
## <a name="sharepoint-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2799">SharePoint Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2799">SharePoint Online features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2800"><a name="BM8_SPOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2800"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-p138">所有 Office 365 計劃都包括 SharePoint Online 服務，但並非所有計劃都支援所有的 SharePoint 功能。下表顯示計劃中是否提供某項功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-p138">All Office 365 plans include the SharePoint Online service, but not all plans support all SharePoint features. The following table shows whether a feature is available in a plan.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-2803">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-2803">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4684"><sup>1</sup> 若要使用資料夾同步處理，您必須擁有 Office 2013 或更新版本 (標準版或專業版)，或是包含 Office 應用程式的 Office 365 訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4684"><sup>1</sup> To use folder sync, you must have Office 2013 or later (Standard or Professional edition) or an Office 365 subscription that includes Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4685">Office 365 商務基本版、Office 365 Enterprise E1 以及 Office 365 教育版 方案並未包含 Office 桌面應用程式訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4685">Office 365 Business Essentials, Office 365 Enterprise E1, and Office 365 Education plans do not include subscriptions to Office desktop applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4686">不過，如果您已安裝 Office 2013 或更新版本，並訂閱上述其中一個方案，就可以使用資料夾同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4686">However, you can use folder sync if you have Office 2013 or later installed and subscribe to one of these plans.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4687"><sup>2</sup> Kiosk 帳戶有限制的 OneDrive 商務功能。.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4687"><sup>2</sup> Kiosk accounts have limited OneDrive for Business functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4688">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4688">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4689">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB of online storage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4689">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB of online storage.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4690"><sup>3</sup> 不支援 Access 2010。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4690"><sup>3</sup> Access 2010 is not supported.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4691"><sup>4</sup> 因為 Kiosk 使用者不能是系統管理員，所以有 Kiosk 使用者的租用戶至少必須有一個企業使用者使用者，才能存取系統管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4691"><sup>4</sup> Because Kiosk users can't be administrators, tenants with Kiosk users need at least one Enterprise user to access the admin center.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4692"><sup>5</sup> SharePoint Online 客戶必須下載並安裝免費的排名模型調整應用程式，才能建立及自訂排名模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4692"><sup>3</sup> SharePoint Online customers need to download and install the free Rank Model Tuning App in order to create and customize ranking models.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4693"><sup>6</sup> 當您使用 eDiscovery 功能時，允許此功能的計劃授權要求會套用至所有屬於 eDiscovery 動作 (搜尋、保留、匯出) 的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4693"><sup>6</sup> When you use eDiscovery features, the licensing requirement for a plan that permits that feature applies to all end users that are part of the eDiscovery action (Search, Hold, Export).</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4694"><sup>7</sup> 已驗證的 SharePoint Online 使用者可以使用多面向導覽存取私用網站集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4694"><sup>7</sup> Authenticated SharePoint Online users can access private site collections with faceted navigation.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4695"><sup>8</sup> Kiosk 使用者不能使用即時磚建立 Office 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4695"><sup>8</sup> Kiosk users cannot create Office documents using live tiles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4696">To create a document, kiosk users must do so from a SharePoint Online site by clicking **New** and then selecting a file type - Word document, Excel workbook, PowerPoint presentation, OneNote notebook, or Excel survey - from the **Create a new file** menu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4696">To create a document, kiosk users must do so from a SharePoint Online site by clicking **New** and then selecting a file type - Word document, Excel workbook, PowerPoint presentation, OneNote notebook, or Excel survey - from the **Create a new file** menu.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4697"><sup>9</sup> 在您的國家/地區中，某些提供者可能被封鎖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4697"><sup>9</sup> Some providers may be blocked in your country/region.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4698"><sup>10</sup> 使用電子郵件與組織外的任何人共用文件、程式庫或網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4698"><sup>8</sup> Sharing a document, library, or site by email with someone outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4699">系統管理員還是能夠將它開啟，但會出現警告訊息，指出它可能在您的國家/地區外進行檔案共用存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4699">Administrators do have the ability to turn it on, but will get a warning message indicating that it could make files shared accessible outside of your country.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4700">嘗試與組織外部的其他人共用的使用者會收到相同的警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4700">Users who attempt to share with someone outside of the organization will receive the same warning message.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4701"><sup>11</sup> Kiosk 帳戶有限制的 OneDrive 商務功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4701"><sup>12</sup> Kiosk accounts have limited OneDrive for Business functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4702">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4702">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-4703">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB or 5 TB of online storage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-4703">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB or 5 TB of online storage.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-5719">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-5719">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span> <br/>
  
>[!NOTE]
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-p151">商務用 Skype Online 獨立方案 2 的授權使用者會得到商務用 Skype 基本用戶端，而非完整的商務用 Skype 用戶端。如果您希望讓使用者擁有商務用 Skype 用戶端，您必須將他們升級為含有該用戶端的授權，例如企業版授權。若要為使用者部署商務用 Skype 用戶端，請參閱[在 Office 365 部署商務用 Skype 用戶端](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-skype-for-business-online/deploy-the-skype-for-business-client-in-office-365)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-p151">Skype for Business Online Standalone Plan 2 licensed users will get the Skype for Business Basic client, not the full Skype for Business client. If you want users to have the Skype for Business client, you will need to upgrade them to a license that includes it, such as an Enterprise-based license. To deploy the Skype for Business client to your users, see [Deploy the Skype for Business client in Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-skype-for-business-online/deploy-the-skype-for-business-client-in-office-365). </span></span><br/>

## <a name="follow-on-wechat"></a><span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-6534">在 WeChat 上關注我們</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-6534">Follow on WeChat</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-6535"><a name="BM10_ProjectOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-6535"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b7d3d-6536">掃描此 QR 碼，在 WeChat 上關注我們的討論區，並取得由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365 的最新更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b7d3d-6536">Scan this QR code to follow discussions on WeChat and get the latest updates for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span>
